Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0025	अक्षांशों को अंश में मापा जाता है।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0025	Latitudes are measured in degrees.	b'^Latitudes/Latitude<n><pl>$ ^are/be<vbser><pres>$ ^measured/measured<adj>/measure<vblex><past>/measure<vblex><pp>$ ^in/in<adv>/in<pr>$ ^degrees/degree<n><pl>$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0026	विषुवत् वृत्त शून्य अंश अक्षांश को दर्शाती है।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0026	The equator represents the zero degree latitude.	b'^The/The<det><def><sp>$ ^equator/equator<n><sg>$ ^represents/represent<vblex><pres><p3><sg>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^zero/zero<num><sg>/zero<n><sg>$ ^degree/degree<n><sg>$ ^latitude/latitude<n><sg>$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0027	चूँकि, विषुवत् वृत्त से दोनों तरफ ध्रुवों के बीच की दूरी पृथ्वी के चारों ओर के वृत्त का एक चैथाई है, अतः इसका माप होगा 360 अंश का 1/4, यानी 90 अंश।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0027	Since the distance from the equator to either of the poles is one-fourth of a circle round the earth, it will measure ¼ th of 360 degrees, i.e. 90.	b'^Since/Since<adv>/Since<cnjsub>/Since<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^distance/distance<n><sg>/distance<vblex><inf>/distance<vblex><pres>/distance<vblex><imp>$ ^from/from<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^equator/equator<n><sg>$ ^to/to<pr>$ ^either/either<adv>/either<cnjcoo>/either<det><ind><sg>/either<prn><qnt><mf><sp>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^poles/pole<n><pl>/polis<n><pl>$ ^is/be<vbser><pres><p3><sg>$ ^one/one<num><sg>/one<prn><dem><mf><sg>$^-/-<guio>$^fourth/fourth<adj><ord>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^a/a<det><ind><sg>$ ^circle/circle<n><sg>/circle<vblex><inf>/circle<vblex><pres>/circle<vblex><imp>$ ^round/round<adv>/round<pr>/round<n><sg>/round<adj><sint>/round<vblex><inf>/round<vblex><pres>/round<vblex><imp>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^earth/earth<n><sg>$^,/,<cm>$ ^it/prpers<prn><subj><p3><nt><sg>/prpers<prn><obj><p3><nt><sg>$ ^will/will<n><sg>/will<vbmod><inf>/will<vbmod><pres>/will<vblex><inf>/will<vblex><pres>/will<vblex><imp>$ ^measure/measure<n><sg>/measure<vblex><inf>/measure<vblex><pres>/measure<vblex><imp>$ \xc2\xbc ^th/th<adj>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^360/360<num>$ ^degrees/degree<n><pl>$^,/,<cm>$ ^i.e./i.e.<abbr>/i.e.<adv>$ ^90/90<num>$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0028	इस प्रकार 90 अंश उत्तरी अक्षांश उत्तर ध्रुव को दर्शाता है तथा 90 अंश दक्षिणी अक्षांश दक्षिण ध्रुव को।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0028	Thus, 90 degrees north latitude marks the North Pole and 90 degrees south latitude marks the South Pole.	b'^Thus/Thus<adv>/Thus<cnjcoo>/Thus<cnjadv>$^,/,<cm>$ ^90/90<num>$ ^degrees/degree<n><pl>$ ^north/north<adv>/north<n><sg>/north<adj><sint>$ ^latitude/latitude<n><sg>$ ^marks/mark<n><pl>/mark<vblex><pres><p3><sg>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^North Pole/North Pole<np><top><sg>$ ^and/and<cnjcoo>$ ^90/90<num>$ ^degrees/degree<n><pl>$ ^south/south<adv>/south<n><sg>/south<adj><sint>$ ^latitude/latitude<n><sg>$ ^marks/mark<n><pl>/mark<vblex><pres><p3><sg>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^South Pole/South Pole<np><top><sg>$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0029	इस प्रकार विषुवत् वृत्त के उत्तर की सभी समानांतर रेखाओं को क्या आप जानते हैं?	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0029	As such, all parallels north of the Latitude equator are called ‘north latitudes.’	b"^As such/As such<adv>$^,/,<cm>$ ^all/all<adv>/all<predet><sp>/all<det><qnt><pl>/all<prn><qnt><mf><sp>$ ^parallels/*parallels$ ^north/north<adv>/north<n><sg>/north<adj><sint>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Latitude/Latitude<n><sg>$ ^equator/equator<n><sg>$ ^are called/be<vblex><pres><p1><pl># called/be<vblex><pres><p2><sg># called/be<vblex><pres><p2><pl># called/be<vblex><pres><p3><pl># called$ \xe2\x80\x98^north/north<adv>/north<n><sg>/north<adj><sint>$ ^latitudes/latitude<n><pl>$^./.<sent>$^\xe2\x80\x99/'<apos>$\n"
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0030	उत्तरी अक्षांश कहा जाता है तथा विषुवत् वृत्त के दक्षिण स्थित सभी अपने स्थान से ध्रुव तारे का कोण मापकर आप समानांतर रेखाओं को दक्षिणी अक्षांश कहा जाता है।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0030	Similarly all parallels south of the equator are called ‘south latitudes.	b'^Similarly/Similarly<adv>$ ^all/all<adv>/all<predet><sp>/all<det><qnt><pl>/all<prn><qnt><mf><sp>$ ^parallels/*parallels$ ^south/south<adv>/south<n><sg>/south<adj><sint>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^equator/equator<n><sg>$ ^are called/be<vblex><pres><p1><pl># called/be<vblex><pres><p2><sg># called/be<vblex><pres><p2><pl># called/be<vblex><pres><p3><pl># called$ \xe2\x80\x98^south/south<adv>/south<n><sg>/south<adj><sint>$ ^latitudes/latitude<n><pl>$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0031	इसलिए प्रत्येक अक्षांश के मान के साथ उसकी दिशा यानी उत्तर या दक्षिण को भी लिखा जाता है।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0031	Generally, this is indicated by the letter ‘N’ or ‘S’.	b"^Generally/Generally<adv>$^,/,<cm>$ ^this/this<det><dem><sg>/this<prn><dem><mf><sg>/this<prn><rel><an><mf><sp>$ ^is/be<vbser><pres><p3><sg>$ ^indicated/indicate<vblex><past>/indicate<vblex><pp>$ ^by/by<adv>/by<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^letter/letter<n><sg>$ \xe2\x80\x98^N/N<abbr>$^\xe2\x80\x99/'<apos>$ ^or/or<cnjcoo>$ \xe2\x80\x98^S/S<abbr>$^\xe2\x80\x99/'<apos>$^./.<sent>$\n"
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0032	उदाहरण के लिए, महाराष्ट्र में चंद्ररूप एवं ब्राज़िल (दक्षिण अमेरिका) में बेलो होरिज़ोंटे दोनों एक ही अक्षांश 20 अंश पर स्थित हैं।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0032	For example, both Chandrapur in Maharashtra  and Belo Horizonte in Brazil  are located on parallels of about 20 latitude.	b'^For example/For example<adv>$^,/,<cm>$ ^both/both<cnjcoo>/both<det><ind><pl>/both<prn><ind><mf><pl>$ ^Chandrapur/*Chandrapur$ ^in/in<adv>/in<pr>$ ^Maharashtra/Maharashtra<np><top><sg>$ ^and/and<cnjcoo>$ ^Belo/*Belo$ ^Horizonte/*Horizonte$ ^in/in<adv>/in<pr>$ ^Brazil/Brazil<np><top><sg>$ ^are/be<vbser><pres>$ ^located/locate<vblex><past>/locate<vblex><pp>$ ^on/on<adv>/on<pr>$ ^parallels/*parallels$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^about/about<adv>/about<pr>$ ^20/20<num>$ ^latitude/latitude<n><sg>$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0033	लेकिन चन्द्रपुर विषुवत् वृत्त के 20 अंश उत्तर में एवं बेलो होरिज़ोंटे विषुवत् वृत्त के 20 अंश दक्षिण में स्थित है।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0033	But the former is 20 north of the equator and the latter is 20 south of it.	b'^But/But<cnjcoo>/But<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^former/former<adj>/former<adv>$ ^is/be<vbser><pres><p3><sg>$ ^20/20<num>$ ^north/north<adv>/north<n><sg>/north<adj><sint>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^equator/equator<n><sg>$ ^and/and<cnjcoo>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^latter/latter<adj>$ ^is/be<vbser><pres><p3><sg>$ ^20/20<num>$ ^south/south<adv>/south<n><sg>/south<adj><sint>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^it/prpers<prn><subj><p3><nt><sg>/prpers<prn><obj><p3><nt><sg>$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0034	इसलिए हम कहते हैं कि चंद्रपुर 20 ° उ. अक्षांश पर तथा बेलो होरिज़ोंटे 20 ° द. अक्षांश पर स्थित है।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0034	We, therefore, say that Chandrapur is situated at 20 N latitude and Belo Horizonte is situated at 20 S latitude.	b'^We/Prpers<prn><subj><p1><mf><pl>$^,/,<cm>$ ^therefore/therefore<adv>/therefore<cnjadv>$^,/,<cm>$ ^say/say<vblex><inf>/say<vblex><pres>/say<vblex><imp>$ ^that/that<cnjsub>/that<det><dem><sg>/that<prn><dem><mf><sg>/that<prn><rel><an><mf><sp>$ ^Chandrapur/*Chandrapur$ ^is/be<vbser><pres><p3><sg>$ ^situated/situated<adj>/situate<vblex><past>/situate<vblex><pp>$ ^at/at<pr>$ ^20/20<num>$ ^N/N<abbr>$ ^latitude/latitude<n><sg>$ ^and/and<cnjcoo>$ ^Belo/*Belo$ ^Horizonte/*Horizonte$ ^is/be<vbser><pres><p3><sg>$ ^situated/situated<adj>/situate<vblex><past>/situate<vblex><pp>$ ^at/at<pr>$ ^20/20<num>$ ^S/S<abbr>$ ^latitude/latitude<n><sg>$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0035	चित्र 2.2 से स्पष्ट है कि जैसे-जैसे हम विषुवत् वृत्त से दूर जाते हैं अक्षांशों का आकार घटता जाता है।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0035	We see in Figure 2.2 that as we move away from the equator, the size of the parallels of latitude decreases.	b'^We/Prpers<prn><subj><p1><mf><pl>$ ^see/see<vblex><inf>/see<vblex><pres>/see<vblex><imp>$ ^in/in<adv>/in<pr>$ ^Figure/Figure<n><sg>/Figure<vblex><inf>/Figure<vblex><pres>/Figure<vblex><imp>$ ^2.2/2.2<num>/2.2<n><file>$ ^that/that<cnjsub>/that<det><dem><sg>/that<prn><dem><mf><sg>/that<prn><rel><an><mf><sp>$ ^as/as<adv>/as<preadv>/as<cnjsub>/as<cnjadv>/as<pr>$ ^we/prpers<prn><subj><p1><mf><pl>$ ^move away/move<vblex><sep><inf># away/move<vblex><sep><pres># away/move<vblex><sep><imp># away$ ^from/from<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^equator/equator<n><sg>$^,/,<cm>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^size/size<n><sg>/size<vblex><inf>/size<vblex><pres>/size<vblex><imp>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^parallels/*parallels$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^latitude/latitude<n><sg>$ ^decreases/decrease<n><pl>/decrease<vblex><pres><p3><sg>$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0036	कर्क रेखा एवं मकर रेखा के बीच के सभी अक्षांशों पर सूर्य वर्ष में एक बार दोपहर में सिर के ठीक ऊपर होता है।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0036	The mid-day sun is exactly overhead at least once a year on all latitudes in between the Tropic of Cancer and the Tropic of Capricorn.	b'^The/The<det><def><sp>$ ^mid/*mid$^-/-<guio>$^day/day<n><sg>$ ^sun/sun<n><sg>/sun<vblex><inf>/sun<vblex><pres>/sun<vblex><imp>$ ^is/be<vbser><pres><p3><sg>$ ^exactly/exactly<adv>$ ^overhead/overhead<adj>$ ^at least/at least<adv>$ ^once a year/once a year<adv>$ ^on/on<adv>/on<pr>$ ^all/all<adv>/all<predet><sp>/all<det><qnt><pl>/all<prn><qnt><mf><sp>$ ^latitudes/latitude<n><pl>$ ^in between/in between<adv>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Tropic/Tropic<n><sg>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^Cancer/Cancer<n><sg>$ ^and/and<cnjcoo>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Tropic/Tropic<n><sg>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^Capricorn/*Capricorn$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0037	इसलिए इस क्षेत्र में सबसे अधिक उष्मा प्राप्त होती है तथा इसे उष्ण कटिबंध कहा जाता है।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0037	This area, therefore, receives the maximum heat and is called the Torrid Zone.	b'^This/This<det><dem><sg>/This<prn><dem><mf><sg>/This<prn><rel><an><mf><sp>$ ^area/area<n><sg>$^,/,<cm>$ ^therefore/therefore<adv>/therefore<cnjadv>$^,/,<cm>$ ^receives/receive<vblex><pres><p3><sg>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^maximum/maximum<adj>/maximum<n><sg>$ ^heat/heat<n><sg>/heat<vblex><inf>/heat<vblex><pres>/heat<vblex><imp>$ ^and/and<cnjcoo>$ ^is called/be<vblex><pres><p3><sg># called$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Torrid/Torrid<adj>$ ^Zone/Zone<n><sg>/Zone<vblex><inf>/Zone<vblex><pres>/Zone<vblex><imp>$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0038	कर्क रेखा तथा मकर रेखा के बाद किसी भी अक्षांश पर दोपहर का सूर्य कभी भी सिर के ऊपर नहीं होता है।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0038	The mid-day sun never shines overhead on any latitude beyond the Tropic of Cancer and the Tropic of Capricorn.	b'^The/The<det><def><sp>$ ^mid/*mid$^-/-<guio>$^day/day<n><sg>$ ^sun/sun<n><sg>/sun<vblex><inf>/sun<vblex><pres>/sun<vblex><imp>$ ^never/never<adv>$ ^shines/shine<n><pl>/shine<vblex><pres><p3><sg>$ ^overhead/overhead<adj>$ ^on/on<adv>/on<pr>$ ^any/any<adv>/any<det><ind><sp>/any<prn><qnt><mf><sp>$ ^latitude/latitude<n><sg>$ ^beyond/beyond<adv>/beyond<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Tropic/Tropic<n><sg>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^Cancer/Cancer<n><sg>$ ^and/and<cnjcoo>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Tropic/Tropic<n><sg>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^Capricorn/*Capricorn$^./.<sent>$\n'
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0039	ध्रुव की तरफ सूर्य की किरणें तिरछी होती जाती हैं।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0039	The angle of the sun’s rays goes on decreasing towards the poles.	b"^The/The<det><def><sp>$ ^angle/angle<n><sg>/angle<vblex><inf>/angle<vblex><pres>/angle<vblex><imp>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^sun/sun<n><sg>/sun<vblex><inf>/sun<vblex><pres>/sun<vblex><imp>$^\xe2\x80\x99/'<apos>$^s/*s$ ^rays/ray<n><pl>$ ^goes on/go<vblex><pres><p3><sg>+on<pr>/go<vblex><pres><p3><sg># on$ ^decreasing/decrease<vblex><pprs>/decrease<vblex><subs>/decrease<vblex><ger>$ ^towards/towards<adv>/towards<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^poles/pole<n><pl>/polis<n><pl>$^./.<sent>$\n"
Hin_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0040	इस प्रकार, उत्तरी गोलार्ध में कर्क रेखा एवं उत्तर ध्रुव वृत्त तथा दक्षिणी गोलार्ध में मकर रेखा एवं दक्षिण ध्रुव वृत्त के बीच वाले क्षेत्र का तापमान मध्यम रहता है।	Eng_Geo_ncert_6stnd_2ch_0040	As such, the areas bounded by the Tropic of Cancer and the Arctic Circle in the Northern Hemisphere, and the Tropic of Capricorn and the Antarctic Circle in the Southern Hemisphere, have moderate temperatures.	b'^As such/As such<adv>$^,/,<cm>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^areas/area<n><pl>$ ^bounded/bound<vblex><pp>/bound<vblex><past>$ ^by/by<adv>/by<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Tropic/Tropic<n><sg>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^Cancer/Cancer<n><sg>$ ^and/and<cnjcoo>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Arctic/Arctic<adj>/Arctic<np><top><sg>$ ^Circle/Circle<n><sg>/Circle<vblex><inf>/Circle<vblex><pres>/Circle<vblex><imp>$ ^in/in<adv>/in<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Northern Hemisphere/Northern hemisphere<n><sg>$^,/,<cm>$ ^and/and<cnjcoo>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Tropic/Tropic<n><sg>$ ^of/of<pr>$ ^Capricorn/*Capricorn$ ^and/and<cnjcoo>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Antarctic/Antarctic<adj>/Antarctic<np><top><sg>$ ^Circle/Circle<n><sg>/Circle<vblex><inf>/Circle<vblex><pres>/Circle<vblex><imp>$ ^in/in<adv>/in<pr>$ ^the/the<det><def><sp>$ ^Southern Hemisphere/Southern hemisphere<n><sg>$^,/,<cm>$ ^have/have<vbhaver><inf>/have<vbhaver><pres>/have<vblex><inf>/have<vblex><pres>/have<vblex><imp>$ ^moderate/moderate<adj>/moderate<n><sg>/moderate<vblex><inf>/moderate<vblex><pres>/moderate<vblex><imp>$ ^temperatures/temperature<n><pl>$^./.<sent>$\n'
